The shampoo and shower gel that costs 7,800 yuan a night is no different from a hotel that costs tens of yuan a night. After taking a shower, my scalp and body were extremely dry. It must be the worst raw material used. The hotel went to great lengths to save costs when purchasing this product. The hair dryer is also an ancient product that has been used for decades. It is still in use after being coated with paste. It is really difficult to use. There is no need to mention the lights, and there is no explanation. It takes a long time to figure out which button corresponds to which light.
2. The service is poor. I have always stayed at the nearby B&W Marriott. This time I went to experience the Sheraton, and there was no service at all.
3. I came to Shanghai for a business trip. Due to something unexpected at noon the next day, I communicated with the hotel the night before to postpone the check-out time from 12 o'clock to 2 o'clock. Since it was past 12 o'clock when I came back to pack my luggage, I needed to make a new room. Card, I already explained the situation when I made the room card, but the hotel front desk specifically said to me, "Will I definitely leave today?" I felt it was strange at the time, as if I had delayed check-out just to stay a little longer.
To sum up, I had a bad experience after staying in this hotel for four nights. I will not stay in this hotel again on business trips in the future. I will also tell my colleagues about the difference between staying in this hotel and there are other options nearby. For those who read this comment, if they spent seven or eight hundred thousand, they might as well stay in other next-level hotels nearby, so don't come here.
